@Septapus help


[12/20/2020 5:40 PM] Septapus#2651
All commands can be used in private messages without the `@Septapus ` prefix.
`@Septapus avatar [@username]` - Returns a big version of your avatar, or a users avatar if provided.
`@Septapus chart <up|down|flat> <vertical message>, <horizontal message>` - Creates a chart trending in the desired direction.
`@Septapus comic [1-10]` - Creates a comic from recent messages, or a number of messages if provided. eg: comic 3
`@Septapus emoji <emoji>` - Returns a big version of an emoji.
`@Septapus help [topic]` - Returns help for a specific topic. Available topics: `chart, comic, emoji, help, pol, reminder, wormhole`
`@Septapus invite` - Returns a URL to add Septapus to your server.
`@Septapus pol [left|right|up|down] <URL|Text|Mention>` - Put an image or text or avatar onto the political spectrum.
`@Septapus reminder <time> <reminder>` - Sets a reminder that is sent after the provided time.
`@Septapus reminderdelete <index>` - Deletes a reminder by index. eg: reminderdelete 0
`@Septapus reminderlist` - List all active reminders.
`@Septapus stats` - Lists bot statistics.
`@Septapus thankyou` - Thank you to all my patrons.
`@Septapus wormhole <info|open|close|send|reply <message>>` - Send messages to other dimensions.

__Fun Commands__
For help & support, check out the [Support Server](https://discord.gg/wrgd3kh)
-rp 8ball <question>
Answers a yes or no question.
-rp coinflip [times=1]
Heads or Tails? Flip a coin multiple times or singularly.
-rp roll [minimum=0] [maximum=100] [times=1]
Rolls a random number once or multiple times within an optional range. You can also roll random tags.
-rp ship [member1] [member2]
Ships two users together, with a score and a cute little heart.
-rp splash [member] [colour1] [colour2] [colour3]
Splash yourself or someone with some colour! Provide up to 3 colours of your choice (Hex codes preferably), otherwise they'll be random colours.
-rp tarot
Get a Tarot reading.
-rp wyr
What Would You Rather do?

All commands can be used in private messages without the `@Septapus ` prefix.
`@Septapus avatar [@username]` - Returns a big version of your avatar, or a users avatar if provided.
`@Septapus chart <up|down|flat> <vertical message>, <horizontal message>` - Creates a chart trending in the desired direction.
`@Septapus comic [1-10]` - Creates a comic from recent messages, or a number of messages if provided. eg: comic 3
`@Septapus emoji <emoji>` - Returns a big version of an emoji.
`@Septapus help [topic]` - Returns help for a specific topic. Available topics: `chart, comic, emoji, help, pol, reminder, wormhole`
`@Septapus invite` - Returns a URL to add Septapus to your server.
`@Septapus pol [left|right|up|down] <URL|Text|Mention>` - Put an image or text or avatar onto the political spectrum.
`@Septapus reminder <time> <reminder>` - Sets a reminder that is sent after the provided time.
`@Septapus reminderdelete <index>` - Deletes a reminder by index. eg: reminderdelete 0
`@Septapus reminderlist` - List all active reminders.
`@Septapus stats` - Lists bot statistics.
`@Septapus thankyou` - Thank you to all my patrons.
`@Septapus wormhole <info|open|close|send|reply <message>>` - Send messages to other dimensions.

[1/8/2023 9:59 PM] mr.owo.
@Septapus help


[1/8/2023 9:59 PM] Septapus#2651
All commands can be used in private messages without the `@Septapus ` prefix.
`@Septapus avatar [@username]` - Returns a big version of your avatar, or a users avatar if provided.
`@Septapus chart <up|down|flat> <vertical message>, <horizontal message>` - Creates a chart trending in the desired direction.
`@Septapus comic [1-10]` - Creates a comic from recent messages, or a number of messages if provided. eg: comic 3
`@Septapus emoji <emoji>` - Returns a big version of an emoji.
`@Septapus help [topic]` - Returns help for a specific topic. Available topics: `chart, comic, emoji, pol, reminder`
`@Septapus invite` - Returns a URL to add Septapus to your server.
`@Septapus pol [left|right|up|down] <URL|Text|Mention>` - Put an image or text or avatar onto the political spectrum.
`@Septapus reminder <time> <reminder>` - Sets a reminder that is sent after the provided time.
`@Septapus reminderdelete <index>` - Deletes a reminder by index. eg: reminderdelete 0
`@Septapus reminderlist` - List all active reminders.
`@Septapus stats` - Lists bot statistics.
`@Septapus thankyou` - Thank you to all my patrons.

[6/24/2023 9:53 PM] Septapus#2651
All commands can be used in private messages without the `@Septapus ` prefix.
`@Septapus avatar [@username]` - Returns a big version of your avatar, or a users avatar if provided.
`@Septapus chart <up|down|flat> <vertical message>, <horizontal message>` - Creates a chart trending in the desired direction.
`@Septapus comic [1-10]` - Creates a comic from recent messages, or a number of messages if provided. eg: comic 3
`@Septapus emoji <emoji>` - Returns a big version of an emoji.
`@Septapus help [topic]` - Returns help for a specific topic. Available topics: `chart, comic, emoji, pol, reminder`
`@Septapus invite` - Returns a URL to add Septapus to your server.
`@Septapus pol [left|right|up|down] <URL|Text|Mention>` - Put an image or text or avatar onto the political spectrum.
`@Septapus reminder <time> <reminder>` - Sets a reminder that is sent after the provided time.
`@Septapus reminderdelete <index>` - Deletes a reminder by index. eg: reminderdelete 0
`@Septapus reminderlist` - List all active reminders.
`@Septapus stats` - Lists bot statistics.
`@Septapus thankyou` - Thank you to all my patrons.
